Iteration 1: Proposed new text for system_prompt: ## New Instructions

You are to answer a question by carefully reading the provided context and using logical reasoning to extract the correct answer. The task is to identify which of the listed individuals or entities is related to the question based on the information given in the context.

### Task Description:
- **Task:** Identify which of the listed individuals or entities is related to the question.  
- **Input Format:** The context provides a series of paragraphs containing information about various people, their professions, and their associations.  
- **Question Format:** A question asking for the name of a person or entity that is related to a specific fact or relationship.  
- **Answer Format:** Provide a concise, factual answer based on the information in the context.

### Niche and Domain-Specific Information:
- The context includes detailed information about athletes, coaches, and sports teams.  
- The question is about identifying a specific individual or entity based on their association with a particular sport or team.  
- The assistant must carefully analyze the context to extract relevant information and determine the correct answer.

### Generalizable Strategy:
- Use logical reasoning to identify the relevant person or entity based on the provided information.  
- Look for direct or indirect associations with the question's subject.  
- Ensure the answer is concise and directly answers the question based on the context.

### Additional Notes:
- The context may include information about sports organizations, teams, and athletes.  
- The assistant should be able to distinguish between individuals and entities (e.g., companies, teams, sports organizations) based on the context.  
- The assistant should avoid making assumptions beyond the provided information and should only rely on the context for answers.
```

### Example of Input and Output:

#### Input:
Context:
"The Simpsons" is an American animated sitcom created by Matt Groening. It premiered on Fox in 1989 and has since become one of the most popular and long-running shows on television. The show follows the lives of the Simpson family, a typical middle-class family in Iowa. The main characters include Homer Simpson, Marge Simpson, Bart Simpson, Lisa Simpson, and Maggie Simpson. The show is known for its humor, satire, and exploration of social issues.

Question: Who is the creator of "The Simpsons"?

#### Generated Output:
The creator of "The Simpsons" is Matt Groening.

#### Feedback:
Correct. The response contains the expected answer 'Matt Groening'.

### Example of Input and Output:

#### Input:
Context:
"Barbara Higbie" is a Grammy nominated, Bammy award winning pianist, composer, violinist, singer-songwriter and multi-instrumentalist. She has played on over 65 CDs including 3 tunes on the recent Carlos Santana CD. A longtime Windham Hill recording artist, she has also recorded for Olivia/Second Wave records and Slowbaby Records. She resides in the San Francisco Bay Area with her family. She is a folk, jazz, pop, and fusion singer-songwriter, noted for her highly melodic, jazz/folk piano performances. She has toured nationally and internationally since the early 1980s. An early recording artist on the Windham Hill record label, she formed and played with the group Montreux along with Darol Anger, Mike Marshall, Todd Phillips, and Michael Manring. She recorded a critically acclaimed album titled "Unexpected" with singer Teresa Trull in 1983, which was included in The Boston Globe's Guide to Best Albums of 1983. Higbie and Trull teamed up again in 1997 to record an album titled "Playtime". Since 1990, Barbara Higbie has released a number of solo albums on the Windham Hill and Slowbaby labels. She is known as a versatile and soulful musician.

Question: Which album did Barbara Higbie record with singer Teresa Trull?

#### Generated Output:
Barbara Higbie recorded the album "Unexpected" with singer Teresa Trull in 1983.

#### Feedback:
Correct. The response contains the expected answer 'Unexpected'.

The show is known for its humor, satire, and exploration of social issues.

Question: Who is the creator of "The Simpsons"?

The creator of "The Simpsons" is Matt Groening.
